Fat Pig Signals
Dear members, i gathered some knowledge about price action, good stuff to read if you're in the mood:)Source:Market Wizards Book by Jack D. SchwagerTA of the financial markets Book by John J. Lee and John J. MurphyDay trading and swing trading Book by Kathy LienBook by RaynerTrading price action trends Book by Al BrooksAdvance Support and Resistance Trading StrategySupport â€“ Area on your chart with potential buying pressureResistance â€“ Area on your chart with potential selling pressure1) The more times Support or Resistance (SR) is tested, the weaker it becomesThe market reverses at Support because there is buying pressure to push the price higher. The buying pressure could be from Institutions, banks, or smart money that trades in large orders.If the market keeps re-testing Support, these orders will eventually be filled. And when all the orders are filled, whoâ€™s left to buy?Higher lows into Resistance usually result in a breakout (ascending triangle). Lower highs into Support usually results in a breakdown (descending triangle).2) Support and Resistance can be dynamicThere are two ways to identify Dynamic SR.You can use:-Moving average.Use the 20 & 50 MA to identify Dynamic SR.Screenshot: http://prntscr.com/ik3iou-Trend line.These are diagonal lines on your chart to identify dynamic SR.Screenshot: http://prntscr.com/ik3je1Treat Support and Resistance as areas on your chart (and not random lines). This applies to both horizontal and dynamic SR.3)How to tell when Support or Resistance will break â€” so you donâ€™t get â€œtrappedâ€.Resistance tends to break in uptrend.For an uptrend to continue, it has to consistently break new highs. Thus, shorting at resistance is a low probability trade.Instead, going long at Support is a better trade.Support tends to break in downtrend.For a downtrend to continue, it has to consistently break new lows. Thus, going long at support isnâ€™t a good idea.But, going short at Resistance is a great idea (Margin).Support and Resistance tend to break when thereâ€™s buildup.Support is an area with potential buying pressure. So, the price should move up quickly, right?Nowâ€¦ what if price didnâ€™t move up and instead, consolidates at Support?What does it mean?A sign of weakness as the bulls couldnâ€™t push the price higher.Perhaps thereâ€™s no buying pressure or, thereâ€™s strong selling pressure. Either way, it doesnâ€™t look good for the bulls and Support is likely to break.Last point based on myself:4) Trading at Support or Resistance gives you favorable risk to rewardIf you've been here for awhile you might remember how i predicted how far DASH could go down.Screenshot: http://prntscr.com/ik3m5jPatience pays in trading. Stop chasing the markets and let price come to you.Mark out your SR areas in advance. Then look for trading opportunities when the price has come to your levels. If the price is elsewhere, stay out.#TAworkswell in crypto!!!

Trader Education The following technical indicators are valuable input for improving your trades_____________________Exponential Moving Average (EMA) CrossoversAn exponential moving average (EMA) is a type of moving average that is similar to a simplemoving average, except that more weight is given to the latest data. It's also known as theexponentially weighted moving average. This type of moving average reacts faster to recentprice changes than a simple moving average. The keypoints of reference are when the EMA crosses over the pricing candlesticks or another EMA. Ifprices are going up and a crossover occurs, that is viewed as a â€œBuyâ€ signal, and vice-versa.View Chart: http://prntscr.com/iluwbp_____________________Relative Strength Index (RSI)The relative strength index (RSI) is a momentum indicator developed by noted technical analystWelles Wilder that compares the magnitude of recent gains and losses over a specified timeperiod to measure speed and change of price movements of a security. It is primarily used toattempt to identify overbought or oversold conditions in the trading of an asset.View chart: http://prntscr.com/ilv4z4_____________________Moving average convergence divergence (MACD)MACD is a trend-following momentum indicator that shows the relationship between two moving averages of prices. The MACD is calculated bysubtracting the 26-day exponential moving average (EMA) from the 12-day EMA. A nine-day EMA of the MACD, called the "signal line", is then plotted on top of the MACD, functioning as a trigger for buy and sell signals.View Chart: http://prntscr.com/ilv8xr_____________________Bollinger BandsDeveloped by famous stock trader John Bollinger, Bollinger Band is plotted two standarddeviations away from a simple moving average.Bollinger Bands are a highly popular technical analysis technique. Many traders believe thecloser the prices move to the upper band, the more overbought the market, and the closer theprices move to the lower band, the more oversold the market. View Chart: http://prntscr.com/ilvgmi

The film won the Academy Award for the Best Adapted Screenplay and got 4 other nominations. Apart from being entertaining, it manages to explain complex financial instruments to the viewers. CryptoCoin Mastery :A lot of people make the same mistakes when they are trading cryptocurrencies. I have found that setting specific goals and monitoring my trading allows me to be the most successful. Here are my top 4 tips that you need to be following when you are trading:1. Never chase after gainsCryptocurrencies are some of the most volatile investments that you can make. One day a coin could jump 20% and then fall all the way back to where it started. If you miss a bounce, it is most likely not a good time to buy into that coin.If I notice that a coin has jumped 10% within an hour, I will disregard it because I consider it a much higher risk trade. Focus on using technical analysis to get into trades before the jumps.2. Never invest in coins that you do not understandSometimes coins are going to go down after you buy them. You are not going to win on every trade. Too many traders get involved trading coins that they do not even understand or believe in. If you do not believe in a coin, how are you going to expect that coin to bounce back? It puts traders in a tough situation they cause them to hold onto coins for too long. Create a watchlist of coins that you believe in and focus on trading those coins. Do not try and pick out the diamond in the rough because some guy on Facebook told you it was the next Bitcoin. Do the research yourself!3. Do not trade to get rich. Trade to build wealthI use a unique trading strategy that focuses on 3%-5% gain and 3% losses. I find that setting strict boundaries for myself allows me to capture gains while eliminating losses. Too many traders are buying coins hoping for a 500% gain in a week. Greed never wins. You have to make the decision yourself but I would suggest not figuring this one out the hard way.4. Sometimes selling is the easiest way to make moneyThe strict guidelines that I set for myself about are a clear example of this. Do not become too attached to coins. It is human nature to hold onto coins for long periods of time. Remember, there is always a winning market. As a trader, you just have to find it.
